Editorial internships at Texas A&M University Press provide experience in proofreading and other entry-level tasks, along with exposure to other facets of scholarly publishing.\n\nDescription of the Internship\n\nInterns, working at least ten hours a week, aid the copyediting department with proofreading, software applications to facilitate electronic publishing, data entry, and similar tasks.  Based on their demonstrated abilities, the interns may be asked to prepare jacket copy, work with illustrations, check permissions, and do other jobs normally done by the inhouse project editors.\n\nSelection and Supervision of the Interns\n\nStudents with an interest in publishing and talent in proofreading and similar tasks are invited to apply for one-semester internships, which may be extended for a second semester, as determined by need and demonstrated skills.  A proofreading test will be given, along with an interview with the editor-in-chief, to be sure the students understand what is expected.  A r\u00e9sum\u00e9 including names and phone numbers of references should be provided. \n\nWhat's in It for the Intern\n\nNo funds are available for pay, but the experience could be invaluable.  Academic credit may be available; check with the undergraduate advisor for information about this.  Even more important are the hard-to-get experience of working with a book publisher and (assuming satisfactory performance) a professional recommendation.\n\n\nBeginning date:  the week of August 27, 2012\n\nApplication deadline:  August 15, 2012\n\nTo apply, schedule an appointment with:\nCecelia Hawkins, Undergraduate Director, English Department \u2013 c-hawkins@tamu.edu\n\nInformation on TAMU Press is available at www.tamupress.com", "type": "link", "id": "153578618025605_100733716737371", "status_type": "shared_story", "icon": "https://fbstatic-a.akamaihd.net/rsrc.php/v2/yD/r/aS8ecmYRys0.gif"}
